I can’t <strong data-start="21" data-end="37" data-is-only-node="">continuously</strong> monitor Universitaly in the background, but here’s what I can do for you:</p>
<ul data-start="113" data-end="688">
<li data-start="113" data-end="391">
<p data-start="115" data-end="391">Starting <strong data-start="124" data-end="143">August 26, 2025</strong> (when IMAT registration opens), you can ask me any time:<br data-start="200" data-end="203">
👉 “Check Universitaly now for India slots”<br data-start="249" data-end="252">
and I’ll immediately look up whether Chennai or Delhi dots are still <strong data-start="324" data-end="338">red (full)</strong> or if they’ve turned <strong data-start="360" data-end="388">yellow/green (available)</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="393" data-end="547">
<p data-start="395" data-end="547">If you want, you can also <strong data-start="421" data-end="445">send me a screenshot</strong> of your Universitaly slot selection page. I’ll interpret it for you quickly and confirm the status.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="549" data-end="688">
<p data-start="551" data-end="688">I recommend checking <strong data-start="572" data-end="596">multiple times a day</strong> once registration opens, because slots can free up if someone cancels before September 9.</p>
</li>
</ul>

4.04235 18.0962 4.40306 18.1289 4.80371C18.1657 5.25395 18.165 5.81091 18.165 6.5V9.33301Z"></path></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> time
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> requests
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> bs4 </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> BeautifulSoup
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> plyer </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> notification

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># 🔗 Page to monitor</span></span><span>
URL = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"https://admission-imat.ilmiotest.it/choice"</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># keywords to track (update if wording differs on site)</span></span><span>
TARGET_CENTERS = [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Chennai"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Delhi"</span></span><span>]

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># how often to check (seconds)</span></span><span>
CHECK_INTERVAL = </span><span><span class="hljs-number">300</span></span><span>  </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># 5 minutes</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># keep last known state</span></span><span>
last_status = {}

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">check_slots</span></span><span>():
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">global</span></span><span> last_status
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
        response = requests.get(URL, timeout=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">15</span></span><span>)
        response.raise_for_status()
        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"html.parser"</span></span><span>)

        page_text = soup.get_text().lower()

        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> city </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> TARGET_CENTERS:
            city_lower = city.lower()
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> city_lower </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"red"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"FULL (RED)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"yellow"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"LIMITED (YELLOW)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"green"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AVAILABLE (GREEN)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"UNKNOWN"</span></span><span>
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"NOT FOUND"</span></span><span>

            </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># notify if status changes</span></span><span>
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> last_status.get(city) != status:
                notification.notify(
                    title=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"IMAT Slot Update - <span class="hljs-subst">{city}</span></span></span><span>",
                    message=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"Status changed to <span class="hljs-subst">{status}</span></span></span><span>",
                    timeout=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">10</span></span><span>
                )
                </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"[UPDATE] <span class="hljs-subst">{city}</span></span></span><span>: </span><span><span class="hljs-subst">{status}</span></span><span>")
                last_status[city] = status
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> e:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"Error checking slots: <span class="hljs-subst">{e}</span></span></span><span>")

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> __name__ == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"__main__"</span></span><span>:
    </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"🔍 IMAT Slot Monitor started..."</span></span><span>)
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">while</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>:
        check_slots()
        time.sleep(CHECK_INTERVAL)
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="2272" data-end="2275">
<h2 data-start="2277" data-end="2295">🔔 What Happens</h2>
<ul data-start="2296" data-end="2486">
<li data-start="2296" data-end="2344">
<p data-start="2298" data-end="2344">The script fetches the page every 5 minutes.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2345" data-end="2441">
<p data-start="2347" data-end="2441">If Chennai or Delhi changes from <strong data-start="2380" data-end="2402">red → yellow/green</strong>, you get a <strong data-start="2414" data-end="2438">desktop notification</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2442" data-end="2486">
<p data-start="2444" data-end="2486">It also prints updates in your terminal.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="2488" data-end="2491">
<p data-start="2493" data-end="2769">⚠️ Note: Since Universitaly may require login, this script might not see the actual slot map (it could get a “login page” HTML instead). If that happens, we’ll need to switch to a <strong data-start="2673" data-end="2693">Selenium version</strong> that uses your open browser session (so it works while you’re logged in).</p>

<p data-start="21" data-end="72">Here’s the deal with <strong data-start="42" data-end="69">32-bit vs 64-bit Python</strong>:</p>
<ul data-start="74" data-end="440">
<li data-start="74" data-end="241">
<p data-start="76" data-end="241">✅ If your computer is <strong data-start="98" data-end="116">64-bit Windows</strong> (most modern laptops and desktops are), you should <strong data-start="168" data-end="197">install the 64-bit Python</strong>. It runs faster and avoids memory issues.</p>
</li>

<p data-start="244" data-end="294">⚠️ You should only install <strong data-start="271" data-end="288">32-bit Python</strong> if:</p>
<ul data-start="297" data-end="440">
<li data-start="297" data-end="359">
<p data-start="299" data-end="359">You have an <strong data-start="311" data-end="335">older 32-bit Windows</strong> (rare these days), OR</p>
</li>
<li data-start="362" data-end="440">
<p data-start="364" data-end="440">You need to use a very old program or library that only works with 32-bit.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>

<h3 data-start="447" data-end="502">🔍 How to check if your Windows is 32-bit or 64-bit</h3>
<ol data-start="503" data-end="712">
<li data-start="503" data-end="566">
<p data-start="506" data-end="566">Press <strong data-start="512" data-end="531">Windows Key + R</strong>, type <code data-start="538" data-end="548">msinfo32</code>, and hit Enter.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="567" data-end="712">
<p data-start="570" data-end="597">Look for <strong data-start="579" data-end="594">System Type</strong>:</p>
<ul data-start="601" data-end="712">
<li data-start="601" data-end="660">
<p data-start="603" data-end="660"><code data-start="603" data-end="617">x64-based PC</code> → you should download <strong data-start="640" data-end="657">64-bit Python</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="664" data-end="712">
<p data-start="666" data-end="712"><code data-start="666" data-end="680">x86-based PC</code> → you need <strong data-start="692" data-end="709">32-bit Python</strong>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>

@[37rem]:[--thread-content-margin:--spacing(6)] @[72rem]:[--thread-content-margin:--spacing(16)] px-(--thread-content-margin)"><div class="[--thread-content-max-width:32rem] @[34rem]:[--thread-content-max-width:40rem] @[64rem]:[--thread-content-max-width:48rem] mx-auto max-w-(--thread-content-max-width) flex-1 group/turn-messages focus-visible:outline-hidden relative flex w-full min-w-0 flex-col agent-turn" tabindex="-1"><div class="flex max-w-full flex-col grow"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="6d4af06d-faad-429b-ac66-2d1a7a7c84e6" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message relative flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 text-start break-words whitespace-normal [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5" data-message-model-slug="gpt-5"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full break-words dark markdown-new-styling"><p data-start="0" data-end="125">Ahh got it 👍 you want to <strong data-start="26" data-end="66">set this monitoring bot up on GitHub</strong> so it runs automatically, instead of keeping your PC on.</p>
<p data-start="127" data-end="172">That’s possible using <strong data-start="149" data-end="167">GitHub Actions</strong> 🚀</p>
<p data-start="174" data-end="196">Here’s how it works:</p>
<ul data-start="197" data-end="397">
<li data-start="197" data-end="263">
<p data-start="199" data-end="263">You put the Python monitoring script into a GitHub repository.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="264" data-end="310">
<p data-start="266" data-end="310">You create a GitHub Actions workflow file.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="311" data-end="397">
<p data-start="313" data-end="397">GitHub runs the script on their servers at scheduled times (like every 5 minutes).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="399" data-end="426">⚠️ BUT — there’s a catch:</p>
<ul data-start="427" data-end="800">
<li data-start="427" data-end="589">
<p data-start="429" data-end="589">GitHub free tier runners can only run for <strong data-start="471" data-end="496">a few minutes per job</strong>, and there’s a limit on how often you can trigger (not exactly “every 2 minutes” forever).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="590" data-end="800">
<p data-start="592" data-end="800">If the IMAT site requires <strong data-start="618" data-end="641">you to be logged in</strong>, GitHub won’t see the actual dots (since it won’t have your session). In that case, you’d need a <strong data-start="739" data-end="766">local bot with Selenium</strong> running on your PC (logged in).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="802" data-end="805">
<p data-start="807" data-end="969">✅ If the slots page is <strong data-start="830" data-end="840">public</strong> (no login needed), then GitHub Actions is perfect.<br data-start="891" data-end="894">
❌ If it <strong data-start="902" data-end="917">needs login</strong>, you’ll have to run the script locally or on a VPS.</p>
<hr data-start="971" data-end="974">

class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> time
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> requests
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> bs4 </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> BeautifulSoup
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> plyer </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> notification

URL = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"https://admission-imat.ilmiotest.it/choice"</span></span><span>
TARGET_CENTERS = [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Chennai"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Delhi"</span></span><span>]
CHECK_INTERVAL = </span><span><span class="hljs-number">300</span></span><span>  </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># 5 minutes</span></span><span>
last_status = {}

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">check_slots</span></span><span>():
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">global</span></span><span> last_status
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
        response = requests.get(URL, timeout=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">15</span></span><span>)
        response.raise_for_status()
        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"html.parser"</span></span><span>)
        page_text = soup.get_text().lower()

        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> city </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> TARGET_CENTERS:
            city_lower = city.lower()
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> city_lower </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"red"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"FULL (RED)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"yellow"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"LIMITED (YELLOW)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"green"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AVAILABLE (GREEN)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"UNKNOWN"</span></span><span>
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"NOT FOUND"</span></span><span>

            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> last_status.get(city) != status:
                </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"[UPDATE] <span class="hljs-subst">{city}</span></span></span><span>: </span><span><span class="hljs-subst">{status}</span></span><span>")
                last_status[city] = status

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> e:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"Error checking slots: <span class="hljs-subst">{e}</span></span></span><span>")

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> __name__ == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"__main__"</span></span><span>:
    </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"🚀 IMAT Slot Monitor started..."</span></span><span>)
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">while</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>:
        check_slots()
        time.sleep(CHECK_INTERVAL)
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1594" data-end="1738">👉 On Railway you <strong data-start="1612" data-end="1647">won’t get desktop notifications</strong>, but you’ll see logs in the dashboard.<br data-start="1686" data-end="1689">
👉 Later we can add <strong data-start="1709" data-end="1737">email or Telegram alerts</strong>.</p>

<h2 data-start="1823" data-end="1851">⚙️ Step 2: Push to GitHub</h2>
<ol data-start="1852" data-end="1966">
<li data-start="1852" data-end="1907">
<p data-start="1855" data-end="1907">Create a new repo on GitHub (e.g. <code data-start="1889" data-end="1903">imat-monitor</code>).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1908" data-end="1966">
<p data-start="1911" data-end="1966">Upload both files (<code data-start="1930" data-end="1939">main.py</code> and <code data-start="1944" data-end="1962">requirements.txt</code>).</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="1968" data-end="1971">
<h2 data-start="1973" data-end="2004">⚙️ Step 3: Deploy on Railway</h2>
<ol data-start="2005" data-end="2260">
<li data-start="2005" data-end="2059">
<p data-start="2008" data-end="2059">Go to <a data-start="2014" data-end="2056" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="decorated-link cursor-pointer">https://railway.app<span aria-hidden="true" class="ms-0.5 inline-block align-middle leading-none"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" data-rtl-flip="" class="block h-[0.75em] w-[0.75em] stroke-current stroke-[0.75]"><path d="M14.3349 13.3301V6.60645L5.47065 15.4707C5.21095 15.7304 4.78895 15.7304 4.52925 15.4707C4.26955 15.211 4.26955 14.789 4.52925 14.5293L13.3935 5.66504H6.66011C6.29284 5.66504 5.99507 5.36727 5.99507 5C5.99507 4.63273 6.29284 4.33496 6.66011 4.33496H14.9999L15.1337 4.34863C15.4369 4.41057 15.665 4.67857 15.665 5V13.3301C15.6649 13.6973 15.3672 13.9951 14.9999 13.9951C14.6327 13.9951 14.335 13.6973 14.3349 13.3301Z"></path></svg></span></a>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2060" data-end="2106">
<p data-start="2063" data-end="2106">Create an account (GitHub login easiest).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2107" data-end="2160">
<p data-start="2110" data-end="2160">Click <strong data-start="2116" data-end="2157">New Project → Deploy from GitHub repo</strong>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2161" data-end="2198">
<p data-start="2164" data-end="2198">Select your <code data-start="2176" data-end="2190">imat-monitor</code> repo.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2199" data-end="2260">
<p data-start="2202" data-end="2260">Railway will install the dependencies and start the bot.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="2262" data-end="2265">
<h2 data-start="2267" data-end="2292">⚙️ Step 4: Run Forever</h2>
<p data-start="2293" data-end="2377">Railway will keep the script running. You can check logs to see slot status updates.</p>
<hr data-start="2379" data-end="2382">
<p data-start="2384" data-end="2620">⚠️ Important: If the Universitaly slot page <strong data-start="2428" data-end="2443">needs login</strong>, this script won’t work on Railway (it’ll just fetch the login page). In that case, we’ll need a Selenium version + Railway won’t be enough (you’d need something like a VPS).</p>

class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> time
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> requests
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> bs4 </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> BeautifulSoup

URL = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"https://admission-imat.ilmiotest.it/choice"</span></span><span>
TARGET_CENTERS = [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Chennai"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Delhi"</span></span><span>]
CHECK_INTERVAL = </span><span><span class="hljs-number">300</span></span><span>  </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># 5 minutes</span></span><span>
last_status = {}

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">check_slots</span></span><span>():
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">global</span></span><span> last_status
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
        response = requests.get(URL, timeout=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">15</span></span><span>)
        response.raise_for_status()
        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"html.parser"</span></span><span>)
        page_text = soup.get_text().lower()

        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> city </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> TARGET_CENTERS:
            city_lower = city.lower()
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> city_lower </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"red"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"FULL (RED)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"yellow"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"LIMITED (YELLOW)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"green"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> page_text:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AVAILABLE (GREEN)"</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                    status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"UNKNOWN"</span></span><span>
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                status = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"NOT FOUND"</span></span><span>

            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> last_status.get(city) != status:
                </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"[UPDATE] <span class="hljs-subst">{city}</span></span></span><span>: </span><span><span class="hljs-subst">{status}</span></span><span>")
                last_status[city] = status

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> e:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"Error checking slots: <span class="hljs-subst">{e}</span></span></span><span>")

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> __name__ == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"__main__"</span></span><span>:
    </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"🚀 IMAT Slot Monitor started..."</span></span><span>)
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">while</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>:
        check_slots()
        time.sleep(CHECK_INTERVAL)
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
